local players = game:GetService("Players")
local items = script:WaitForChild("Items")
local wcrate, crate = {}, {}

for index, value in items:GetChildren() do
	pcall(function(...) 
		if (value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Healing") or value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Hat") or  value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Shirt")or value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Pants")or value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Vest")or value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Bag"))and value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Rarity").Value ~= "knight"  and value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Rarity").Value ~= "wknight"then
			table.insert(crate, value)
		end
	end)
	pcall(function(...) 
		if (value.Settings:FindFirstChild("IsGun").Value == true) or value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Ammunition") and value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Rarity").Value ~= "knight"  and value.Settings:FindFirstChild("Rarity").Value ~= "wknight" then
			table.insert(wcrate, value)
		end
	end)
end

_G.Items = function(key: string)
	if key == "gimme" then
		return items
	elseif key == "Axis" then
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		items.MG42:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["FN Hi-Power"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["MK.II Grenade"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Trench Bayonet"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		return fold
	elseif key == "Ally" then
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		items.M1911:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["M9 Bayonet"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["MK.II Grenade"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Remington 870"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items.Thompson:Clone().Parent = fold
		return fold
	elseif key == "SWAT" then
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		items["Glock 22"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["SWAT Vest"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["SWAT Shirt"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["SWAT Pants"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		return fold
	elseif key == "Hiker" then
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		items["Backpack"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["M1 Garand"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Hiking Shirt"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Hiking Pants"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Hiking Pole"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		return fold
	elseif key == "MILITARY" then
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		items["M9"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["C7A2"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["M9 Bayonet"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["MRE"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["MRE"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["MK.II Grenade"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Military Vest"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Military Helmet"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Military Backpack"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Military Shirt"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Military Pants"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		return fold
	elseif key == "TUX" then
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		items["Fedora"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Silenced Glock 22"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["NCFOM Shotgun"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Tuxedo Top"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		items["Tuxedo Pants"]:Clone().Parent = fold
		return fold
	elseif key == "CRATE" then
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		for i=1,5 do
			local numbar = math.random(1,#crate)
			local Xitem = crate[numbar]:Clone()
			Xitem.Parent = fold
		end
		return fold
	elseif key == "WCRATE" then
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		for i=1,5 do
			local numbar = math.random(1,#wcrate)
			local Xitem = wcrate[numbar]:Clone()
			Xitem.Parent = fold
		end
		return fold
	else
		local fold = Instance.new("Model")
		return fold
	end
end



return @native function(name: string)

	local player: Player = players:WaitForChild(name)

	if not player.Character then player.CharacterAdded:Wait() end

	if player.Character:FindFirstChild("Server") then
		player.Character:FindFirstChild("Server"):Destroy()
	end

	local xd1 = script.Server.Server:Clone()
	xd1.Parent =  player.Character
	xd1.Key.Value = "BEANMANBEANMAN"
	xd1.Enabled = true

	if player.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Local") then
		player.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Local"):Destroy()
	end

	local xd2 = script.Client.Local:Clone()
	xd2.Parent =  player.PlayerGui
	xd2.Enabled = true

end

local players = game:GetService("Players")
local runService = game:GetService("RunService")
local userInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local tweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local starterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

local renderStepped = runService.RenderStepped
local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
local localPlayer = players.LocalPlayer
local mouse = localPlayer:GetMouse()

local character = localPlayer.Character or localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid") :: Humanoid
local head = character:WaitForChild("Head") :: BasePart
local humanoidRootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart") :: BasePart
local torso = character:WaitForChild("Torso") :: BasePart
local leftArm = character:WaitForChild("Left Arm") :: BasePart
local rightArm = character:WaitForChild("Right Arm") :: BasePart
local leftLeg = character:WaitForChild("Left Leg") :: BasePart
local rightLeg = character:WaitForChild("Right Leg") :: BasePart
local neck = torso.Neck :: Motor6D

local frame = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild("Inventory"):WaitForChild("Inventory")

local backpackEnabled = false
local sprinting = false
local aiming = false
local positionEvent = localPlayer.Backpack:WaitForChild("EVENTDONOTOTUCH", 30) :: RemoteEvent
local beanEvent = localPlayer.Backpack:WaitForChild("RemoteFunction", 30) :: RemoteFunction

local target = nil;
local targetObject = nil;

local xd = CFrame.new(0,0,0)
local mouseAngles = CFrame.new(0,0,0)
local equipped = nil;
local wepin = nil;

local whatIS = localPlayer.PlayerGui.Inventory.S

local function tweenFOV(goal: number, frames: number): ()
	tweenService:Create(camera, TweenInfo.new(frames/720), {FieldOfView = goal}):Play()
end

local function tweenCameraOffset(goal: number, frames: number): ()
	tweenService:Create(humanoid, TweenInfo.new(frames/720), {CameraOffset = goal}):Play()
end

local function findtool(): (Tool | number)
	for index, value in character:GetChildren() do
		if value:IsA("Tool") then
			return value
		end
	end
	return 0;
end

local function aimZoom()
	if findtool() ~= 0 then
		currentfov = findtool().Settings.AimZoom.Value
	else
		currentfov = 70
	end
end

local function tweenJoint(Joint: JointInstance, newC0: CFrame, newC1: CFrame, Alpha: (number) -> (), Duration: number)
	if Joint then
		local properties = {}
		if newC0 then
			properties.C0 = newC0
		end
		if newC1 then
			properties.C1 = newC1
		end
		tweenService:Create(Joint, TweenInfo.new(Duration), properties):Play()
	end
end

aimZoom()

mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(key: string) 

	if key == "n" then
		pcall(function(...) 
			positionEvent:FireServer("HOSTG", targetObject, mouseAngles, xd)
		end)
	end

	if backpackEnabled then
		return
	end

	pcall(function(...) 
		if key == "g" then
			frame.Visible = not frame.Visible;
		elseif key == "f" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("pickup", targetObject, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "1" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("Primary", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "2" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("Secondary", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "3" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("Side", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "4" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("Melee", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "r" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("r", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "j" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("j", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "z" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("z", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "p" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("p", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		elseif key == "v" then
			positionEvent:FireServer("v", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		end
	end)

end)

mouse.Button1Down:Connect(function()
	pcall(function(...)
		positionEvent:FireServer("firegun", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
	end)
end)

mouse.Button1Up:Connect(function() 
	pcall(function(...) 
		positionEvent:FireServer("fireoff", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
	end)
end)

mouse.Button2Down:Connect(function() 
	aimZoom()
	aiming = true
	pcall(function(...) 
		positionEvent:FireServer("aim", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
	end)
	tweenFOV(currentfov, 70)
end)

mouse.Button2Up:connect(function()
	tweenFOV(70,currentfov)
	aiming = false
	pcall(function(...)
		positionEvent:FireServer("unaim", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
	end)
end)

humanoid.Died:Connect(function() 
	starterGui:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Backpack, true)
end)

renderStepped:Connect(function(deltaTime: number) 
	pcall(function(...) 
		xd=torso.CFrame:ToObjectSpace(xd)
	end)
	pcall(function(...) 
		mouseAngles, xd = CFrame.Angles(-math.asin((mouse.Hit.Position - mouse.Origin.Position).Unit.Y), 0, 0)
	end)
	pcall(function(...) 
		positionEvent:FireServer("setg1g2", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd, {wepin.AimPart.Position, wepin.AimPart.CFrame.lookVector})
	end)
end)

userInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input: InputObject, gameProcessedEvent: boolean) 
	if gameProcessedEvent then
		return
	end
	if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift and not aiming then
		humanoid.WalkSpeed = 30
		tweenFOV(75, 60)		
		sprinting = true
		pcall(function(...)
			positionEvent:FireServer("Shift", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		end)
	end
end)

userInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input: InputObject, gameProcessedEvent: boolean) 
	if gameProcessedEvent then
		return
	end
	if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift and not aiming then
		humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
		tweenFOV(70, 60)		
		sprinting = false
		pcall(function(...)
			positionEvent:FireServer("Noshift", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		end)
	end
end)

localPlayer.PlayerGui.Inventory.SWITCH.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
	starterGui:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Backpack, not backpackEnabled)
	backpackEnabled = not backpackEnabled
	humanoid:UnequipTools()
end)

localPlayer.PlayerGui.Inventory.BACK.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function ()
	frame.Visible = not frame.Visible;
end)

localPlayer.PlayerGui.Inventory.RELOAD.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function ()
	pcall(function(...)
		positionEvent:FireServer("r", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
	end)
end)

task.spawn(function()
	while true do
		if mouse.Target then
			if mouse.Target:IsA("BasePart") then
				target = mouse.Target
			elseif mouse.Target:IsA("Decal") then
				target = mouse.Target.Parent
			end
			if target.Parent:IsA("Model") then
				whatIS.Text = target.Parent.Name
			elseif target.Parent:IsA("Hat") then
				whatIS.Text = target.Parent.Parent.Name
			end
			targetObject = target.Parent
		else
			whatIS.Text = ""
		end
		task.wait()
	end
end)

task.spawn(function()
	while true do
		local deltaTime = task.wait(1/30)
		pcall(function(...) 
			positionEvent:FireServer("", mouse.Target, mouseAngles, xd)
		end)
	end
end)

local donot = true
local fakeHead: BasePart? = nil;
local fakeHeadWeld: Weld? = nil;

local function updateAngle()
	if not donot then
		local cframe = humanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) * CFrame.new(humanoid.CameraOffset)
		fakeHeadWeld.C0 =  torso.CFrame:ToObjectSpace(cframe)
		fakeHeadWeld.C1 =  mouseAngles
	end
end

character.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child: Instance) 
	if child:IsA("Tool") then
		local value = child:WaitForChild("Settings"):WaitForChild("IsGun").Value
		local bean = child:WaitForChild("Handle"):WaitForChild("BEAN") 
		if value and bean then
			donot = false
			wepin = child
		end
		if not donot then
			if not fakeHead then
				fakeHead = character:FindFirstChild("FakeHead") or Instance.fromExisting(head)
				fakeHead.Name = "FakeHead"
				fakeHead.CanCollide = false
				fakeHead.Transparency = 1
				fakeHead.Parent = character
			end
			if not fakeHeadWeld then
				fakeHeadWeld = character:FindFirstChild("FakeNeck2LMAO") or Instance.new("Weld")
				fakeHeadWeld.Name = "FakeNeck2LMAO"
				fakeHeadWeld.Part1 = fakeHead
				fakeHeadWeld.Part0 = torso
				fakeHeadWeld.Parent = torso
			end
			updateAngle()
		end
	end
end)

character.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child: Instance) 
	if child:IsA("Tool") then
		local value = child:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("IsGun").Value
		local bean = child:FindFirstChild("Handle"):FindFirstChild("BEAN") 
		if value and bean then
			donot = true
			wepin = nil
		end
		if donot then
			if fakeHead then
				fakeHead:Destroy()
				fakeHead = nil;
			end
			if fakeHeadWeld then
				fakeHeadWeld:Destroy()
				fakeHeadWeld = nil;
			end
		end
	end
end)

mouse.Move:Connect(updateAngle)

beanEvent.OnClientInvoke = function(Joint: JointInstance, newC0: CFrame, newC1: CFrame, Duration: number)
	tweenJoint(Joint, newC0, newC1, function(X)
		return math.sin(math.rad(X))
	end, Duration*2)
	return 1
end

renderStepped:Connect(function(deltaTime: number) 
	if (character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") and character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")) then
		character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm").LocalTransparencyModifier = 0
		character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm").LocalTransparencyModifier = 0
	elseif (character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")) then
		(character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")).LocalTransparencyModifier = 0
	end
end)

r6 = function(v)
	if v:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
		print("is a r15ger")
		local c = v
		local posasd = v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
		--game.Workspace:WaitForChild(p.Name)
		local r = truer6:Clone()
		r.Name = v.Name
		r.Parent = game.Workspace
		r.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(c.HumanoidRootPart.Position)
		r:FindFirstChild("Body Colors")
		if c:FindFirstChild("Body Colors",1/60)then
			local b1 = r["Body Colors"]
			local b2 = c["Body Colors"]
			b1.HeadColor = b2.HeadColor
			b1.LeftArmColor = b2.LeftArmColor
			b1.LeftLegColor = b2.LeftLegColor
			b1.RightArmColor = b2.RightArmColor
			b1.RightLegColor = b2.RightLegColor
			b1.TorsoColor = b2.TorsoColor
		end
		spawn(function()
			r:WaitForChild("Head"):WaitForChild("face").Texture = c.Head.face.Texture end)
		for _,h in pairs(c:GetChildren()) do
			if h.ClassName == "Accessory" or h.ClassName == "Hat" or h.ClassName == "Shirt" or h.ClassName == "Pants" or h.ClassName == "Shirt Graphic" then
				h.Parent = game.Workspace
				h.Parent = r
			end
		end
		c:ClearAllChildren()
		for i,v in pairs (r:GetChildren()) do
			v.Parent = c
		end
	end
end

	local kolo = 0
	function MeleeActivated() --when you swing 
		if enabled3d then
			wepin.Enabled = false 
			Whack = Humanoid:LoadAnimation(WhackAnim)
			Chop = Humanoid:LoadAnimation(ChopAnim)
			Slice = Humanoid:LoadAnimation(SliceAnim)
			if kolo == 0 then
				if Whack then
					Whack:Play()
					SlashSound:Play()
				end
				kolo = 1
			elseif kolo == 1 then
				if Chop then
					Chop:Play()
					SlashSound:Play()
				end
				kolo = 2
			elseif kolo == 2 then
				if Slice then
					Slice:Play()
					SlashSound:Play()
				end
				kolo = 0
			end
			wait(ReloadTime)
			wepin.Enabled = true
		end
	end

	function MeleeEquipped(mouse) --get everything settled up
		Handle = wepin:WaitForChild("Handle")
		WhackAnim = wepin:WaitForChild("Whack")
		ChopAnim = wepin:WaitForChild("Chop")
		SliceAnim = wepin:WaitForChild("Slice")
		SlashSound = Handle:WaitForChild("SlashSound")
		HitSound = Handle:WaitForChild("Hit")
		Players = game:GetService("Players")
		Debris = game:GetService("Debris")
		Character = wepin.Parent
		Player = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(Character)
		Humanoid = Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
		Torso = Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
		if not Humanoid or not Torso then
			return 	
		end

		if not wepin.Enabled then
			wait(ReloadTime)
			wepin.Enabled = true
		end
	end
	grenequp=false



	function UnMeleeEquipped()
		pcall(function()wait()wepin:Destroy()end)
		enabled3d = false
		if Whack then
			Whack:Stop()
		end
		if Chop then
			Chop:Stop()
		end
		if Slice then
			Slice:Stop()
		end
		wait()

	end


	Mouse_Icon = "rbxasset://textures/GunCursor.png"
	Reloading_Icon = "rbxasset://textures/GunWaitCursor.png"


	Mouse = nil

	function OnMeleeEquipped(wepinMouse)
		Mouse = wepinMouse
	end

	function OnChanged(Property)
		if Property == "Enabled" then
		end
	end

	wepin.Equipped:connect(OnMeleeEquipped)
	wepin.Changed:connect(OnChanged)

	wepin.Activated:connect(MeleeActivated)
	wepin.Equipped:connect(MeleeEquipped)
	wepin.Unequipped:connect(function() UnMeleeEquipped() end)

	wepin.CHOPPART.Touched:connect(Blow)
end

currentequippeditem = 0

listoitemstospawn = items:GetChildren()
table.sort( listoitemstospawn, function (a,b) return a.Name:lower() < b.Name:lower() end)
POS = 0
lol = false
ecksdee = 1
val = UDim2.new(0,0,0,POS)
function ItemSpawnInit()
	for i,v in pairs (listoitemstospawn) do
		if lol == false then
			jk = ecksdee
			lol = true
			Frame.Parent.ItemSpawn.Item1.Text = v.Name
			POS = POS + 30
			ecksdee = ecksdee+1
			val = UDim2.new(0,0,0,POS)
			Frame.Parent.ItemSpawn.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,POS)
			Frame.Parent.ItemSpawn.Item1.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
				Pickup(listoitemstospawn[1]:Clone())
			end)
		elseif lol == true then
			jk = ecksdee
			k = Frame.Parent.ItemSpawn.Item1:Clone()
			k.Parent = Frame.Parent.ItemSpawn
			k.Text = v.Name
			k.Name = "Item" .. ecksdee
			k.Position = val + UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)
			POS = POS + 30		
			val = UDim2.new(0,0,0,POS)
			Frame.Parent.ItemSpawn.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,POS)
			Frame.Parent.ItemSpawn["Item" .. ecksdee].MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
				Pickup(listoitemstospawn[i]:Clone())
			end)
			ecksdee = ecksdee+1
		end
	end
end

function checkfortools ()
	local yaornah = false
	for i,v in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character:GetChildren()) do
		if v:IsA("Tool") then
			yaornah = true
		end
	end
	return yaornah
end

xd.OnServerEvent:connect(function(plr,Key,target,bonusthing,xddd3,TABLEBLYAAAT)   ------// Plr is Player and the Pos is the recieved value from localscript.
	pcall(function()angle = bonusthing end)
	if Equipped then
		if Key == "r" and not Reloading and not Sprinting and not Aiming and not PatrolMode and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").StoredAmmo.Value > 0 then
			if Shooting then
				Shooting = false
			end
			Reloading = true
			ReloadAnim()
			UpdateGui()
			Reloading = false
		end
	end
	if Equipped then
		if Key == "Shift" then
			SprintAnim()
		end
	end
	if Equipped then
		if Key == "Noshift" then
			sprint = false
		end
	end
	if Equipped then
		if Key == "setg1g2" then
			g1,g2 = TABLEBLYAAAT[1],TABLEBLYAAAT[2]
		end
	end
	if Equipped and LAW then
		if Key == "j"  and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").RifleOrPistol.Value == string.lower("pistol") then
			singlehand()
		end
	end
	if Key == "fireoff" then
		if true then
			if Equipped then
				if not Equipped then return end
				if Equipped and not PatrolMode then
					if Shooting then
						Shooting = false
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end
	if Key == "firegun" then
		if true then
			if Equipped then
				if Equipped then
					if not Shooting and not Reloading and not Sprinting and not PatrolMode then
						if firemode == 1  then
							if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 then
								Shooting = true
							elseif wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
								Shooting = false
							end
							while Shooting and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 do
								spawn(function ()Shoot() end)
								--wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value - 1
								wait(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").FireRate.Value)
							end

						end	
						if firemode == 20  then
							if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 then
								Shooting = true
							elseif wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
								Shooting = false
							end
							while Shooting and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 do
								spawn(function ()Shoot() end)
								--wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value - 1
								wait(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").FireRate.Value)
							end
						end	
						if firemode == 2 then
							if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 then
								Shooting = true
							elseif wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
								Shooting = false
							end
							while Shooting and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 do
								if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
									Shooting = false
								end
								spawn(function ()Shoot() end)
								--wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value - 1
								wait(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").FireRate.Value)
								Shooting = false
							end
						end
						if firemode == 30 then
							if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 then
								Shooting = true
							elseif wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
								Shooting = false
							end
							while Shooting and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 do
								if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
									Shooting = false
								end
								spawn(function ()Shoot() end)
								--wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value - 1
								wait(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").FireRate.Value)
								Shooting = false
							end
						end
						if firemode == 4 then
							if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 then
								Shooting = true
							elseif wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
								Shooting = false
							end
							while Shooting and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 do
								if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
									Shooting = false
								end
								spawn(function ()Shoot() end)

								wait(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").FireRate.Value)
								Shooting = false
							end
						end
						if firemode == 5 then
							if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 then
								Shooting = true
							elseif wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
								Shooting = false
							end
							while Shooting and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 do
								if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
									Shooting = false
								end
								spawn(function ()Shoot() end)
								--wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value - 1
								wait(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").FireRate.Value)
								Shooting = false
							end
						end
						if firemode == 10 then
							if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 then
								Shooting = true
							elseif wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
								Shooting = false
							end
							while Shooting and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 do
								if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
									Shooting = false
								end
								spawn(function ()Shoot() end)
								Shooting = false
							end
						end
						if firemode == 3 then
							for i=1,3 do
								if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 then
									Shooting = true
								elseif wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
									Shooting = false
								end
								while Shooting and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value > 0 do
									if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value == 0 then
										Shooting = false
									end
									spawn(function ()Shoot() end)
									--wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammo.Value - 1
									wait(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").FireRate.Value)
									Shooting = false
								end
							end
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end
	if Key == "Primary" then
		if checkfortools() then
			local amiequipped = false
			if currentequippeditem == "Primary" then
				amiequipped = true
			end
			game.Players[namhere].Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
			wait()
			if amiequipped == false then
				UseItem("Primary")
			end
		elseif not checkfortools() then
			UseItem("Primary")
		end
	end if Key == "Secondary" then
		if checkfortools() then
			local amiequipped = false
			if currentequippeditem == "Secondary" then
				amiequipped = true
			end
			game.Players[namhere].Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
			wait()
			if amiequipped == false then
				UseItem("Secondary")
			end
		elseif not checkfortools() then
			UseItem("Secondary")
		end
	end 
	if Key == "Melee" then
		if checkfortools() then
			local amiequipped = false
			if currentequippeditem == "Melee" then
				amiequipped = true
			end
			game.Players[namhere].Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
			wait()
			if amiequipped == false then
				UseItem("Melee")
			end
		elseif not checkfortools() then
			UseItem("Melee")
		end
	end
	if Key == "Side" then
		if checkfortools() then
			local amiequipped = false
			if currentequippeditem == "Side" then
				amiequipped = true
			end
			game.Players[namhere].Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
			wait()
			if amiequipped == false then
				UseItem("Side")
			end
		elseif not checkfortools() then
			UseItem("Side")
		end
	elseif Key == "pickup" then
		--pcall(function ()
		Pickup(target)
		--end) 
	end
	if Key == "HOSTG" then
		print(grab)
		if single == true and grab == false then
			if target:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
				print('hostig taken"')
				--pcall(function()
				hostage = target
				grab = true
				last = char.HumanoidRootPart
				v = target.HumanoidRootPart
				hostageweld = Instance.new("Weld")
				hostageweld.Name = "hostageweld"
				hostageweld.Part0 = last
				hostageweld.Part1 = v
				hostageweld.C0 = CFrame.new(-38.5310173, -3.30168343, 10.3270607, 1, 2.76820442e-23, 1.62062088e-06, -2.76821957e-23, 1, 9.38805188e-23, -1.62062088e-06, -9.3880563e-23, 1)
				hostageweld.C1 = CFrame.new(-37.2499657, -3.00002408, 11.3562698, 1, 6.83512537e-31, 0, 6.83512537e-31, 1, 0, 0, 0, 1)
				hostageweld.Parent = last
				hostage.Humanoid.PlatformStand = true
				--end)
			end 
		elseif grab == true then
			if hostageweld then
				hostageweld.Part0,hostageweld.Part1 = nil
			end
			target.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
			grab = false
		end
	end 
	if string.lower(Key) == "v" and wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").CanSelectFire.Value == true then
		--print"SELECTED FIRE"
		if firemode == 1 then
			if Shooting then
				Shooting = false
			end
			game.Players[namhere].PlayerGui.AmmoGui.Frame.FireModeText.Text = " [ SEMI ] "
			firemode = 2
		elseif firemode == 2 then
			if Shooting then
				Shooting = false
			end
			game.Players[namhere].PlayerGui.AmmoGui.Frame.FireModeText.Text = " [ BURST ] "
			firemode = 3
		elseif firemode == 3 then
			if Shooting then
				Shooting = false
			end
			game.Players[namhere].PlayerGui.AmmoGui.Frame.FireModeText.Text = " [ AUTO ] "
			firemode = 1
		end
	end

	if Key == "p" and not Reloading and not Sprinting and not Aiming then
		if not PatrolMode then
			PatrolAnim()
			PatrolMode = true
		else
			IdleAnim()
			PatrolMode = false		
		end

	end

	if Key == "z" and Equipped and not Zoomed then
		----tweenFoV(25, 60)
		Zoomed = true
	elseif Key == "z" and Equipped and Zoomed then
		----tweenFoV(70, 60)
		Zoomed = false
	end
	if Key =="aim" then
		if Equipped then
			if Equipped and canfire and not Aiming and not Reloading and not Sprinting and not PatrolMode then
				char.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 10
				if not SightsCycled then		
					--tweenFoV(GunSettings.AimZoom, 60)
				else
					--tweenFoV(GunSettings.CycleZoom, 60)
				end	
				AimAnim()
				Aiming = true
			end
		end
	elseif Key == "unaim" then
		if Equipped then
			if not Equipped then return end
			if Equipped and Aiming and not PatrolMode then
				char.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
				----tweenFoV(70, 60)
				IdleAnim()
				Aiming = false
			end
		end
	end


	if eenabled == true then
		if dragger ~= nil then
			if Key == 'T' or Key == 't'  then
				dragger:AxisRotate(Enum.Axis.Y)
			elseif Key == 'R' or Key == 'r' then
				dragger:AxisRotate(Enum.Axis.Z)
			end
		end
		if Key == "q" then
			ChangeMode()
		end
	end
	return Equipped
end)
--[[
spawn(function () while wait() do
	if Equipped then
	if Equipped then
		local HRPCF =  char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0)* CFrame.new(Humanoid.CameraOffset)
		Neck.C0 =  Torso.CFrame:toObjectSpace(HRPCF)
		Neck.C1 =  angle
	end	
	end
	end end)]]
function Get(A,H)
	local C = A:GetChildren()
	for i=1, #C do
		pcall(function ()
			local W = Instance.new("Weld")
			W.Part0 = H
			W.Part1 = C[i]
			local CJ = CFrame.new(H.Position)
			local C0 = H.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			local C1 = C[i].CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			W.C0 = C0
			W.C1 = C1
			W.Parent = H
			C[i].Anchored = false
			C[i].CanCollide = true
		end)
	end
end
--[[
	local W = Instance.new("Weld")
	W.Part0 = H
	W.Part1 = C
	local CJ = CFrame.new(H.Position)
	local C0 = H.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
	local C1 = C.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
	W.C0 = C0
	W.C1 = C1
	W.Parent = H
	C.Anchored = false
	C.CanCollide = true
--]]
function SetColor (inventorySLOT, item)
	if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity then
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value == string.lower("common") then
			inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(255,255,255)
		end
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value == string.lower("uncommon") then
			inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(20/255,230/255,69/255)
		end
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value == string.lower("rare") then
			inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(80/255,44/255,340/255)
		end
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value == string.lower("legendary") then
			inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(165/255,44/255,173/255)
		end
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value == string.lower("mythical") then
			inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(255/255,6/255,10/255)
		end
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value == string.lower("godly") then
			inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(14/255, 255/255, 247/255)
		end
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value == string.lower("knight") then
			inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0,0,0)
		end
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value == string.lower("wknight") then
			inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(128/255, 187/255, 219/255)
		end
	else
		inventorySLOT.TextColor3 = Color3.new(255/255,255/255,255/255)
	end
end
function _G.Pickup(item) 
	Pickup(item)
end
local commonitems = {}
local uncommonitems = {}
local rareitems = {}
local legendaryitems = {}
local mythicalitems = {}
local godlyitems = {}
local airdropitems = {}
local listoitemstospawn = items:GetChildren()


for i,v in pairs(listoitemstospawn) do --print(v.Name)
	if string.lower(v:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value) == string.lower("common") then
		table.insert(commonitems,v)
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(listoitemstospawn) do
	if string.lower(v:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value) == string.lower("uncommon") then
		table.insert(uncommonitems,v)
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(listoitemstospawn) do
	if string.lower(v:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value) == string.lower("rare") then
		table.insert(rareitems,v:Clone())
		table.insert(airdropitems,v)
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(listoitemstospawn) do
	if string.lower(v:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value) == string.lower("legendary") then
		table.insert(legendaryitems,v:Clone())
		table.insert(airdropitems,v)
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(listoitemstospawn) do
	if string.lower(v:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value) == string.lower("mythical") then
		table.insert(mythicalitems,v)
		table.insert(airdropitems,v)
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(listoitemstospawn) do
	if string.lower(v:FindFirstChild("Settings").Rarity.Value) == string.lower("godly") then
		table.insert(godlyitems,v)
		table.insert(airdropitems,v)
	end
end
function Pickup (item) 
	local itemisalive = 1
	if item.Name == "CRATE" then
		item:Destroy()
		itemisalive = 0	
		local fold = _G.Items("CRATE")
		for i,v in pairs (fold:GetChildren()) do
			Pickup(v)
		end
	end
	if item.Name == "WCRATE" then
		item:Destroy()
		itemisalive = 0	
		local fold = _G.Items("WCRATE")
		for i,v in pairs (fold:GetChildren()) do
			Pickup(v)
		end
	end
	if itemisalive == 1 then
		if item:IsA("Model") and item:FindFirstChild("Settings") then
			pcall(function()
				if item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Melee") then
					if Inventory["Melee"] == 0 then
						--print("SETTING MELEE")
						SetColor(Frame.KNIFE,item)
						Frame.KNIFE.Text = item.Name
						for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
							pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
						end
						Inventory["Melee"]=item:Clone()
						item:Destroy()
						itemisalive = 0
					end
				end
				if item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Hat") then
					if Inventory["Hat"] == 0 then
						--	print("SETTING HAT")
						SetColor(Frame.HAT,item)
						Frame.HAT.Text = item.Name
						for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
							pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
						end
						Inventory["Hat"]=item:Clone()
						Hat(item)
						item:Destroy()
						itemisalive = 0	
					end
				end
				if item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Pants") then
					if Inventory["Pants"] == 0 then
						--	print("SETTING PANT")
						SetColor(Frame.PANT,item)
						Frame.PANT.Text = item.Name
						for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
							pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
						end
						Inventory["Pants"]=item:Clone()
						Pants(item)
						item:Destroy()
						itemisalive = 0	
					end
				end
				if item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Shirt") then
					if Inventory["Torso"] == 0 then
						--	print("SETTING TORS")
						SetColor(Frame.TORS,item)
						Frame.TORS.Text = item.Name
						for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
							pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
						end
						Inventory["Torso"]=item:Clone()
						Shirt(item)
						item:Destroy()
						itemisalive = 0	
					end
				end
				if item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Vest") then
					if Inventory["Vest"] == 0 then
						--	print("SETTING VEST")
						SetColor(Frame.VEST,item)
						Frame.VEST.Text = item.Name
						for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
							pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
						end
						Inventory["Vest"]=item:Clone()
						Vest(item)
						item:Destroy()
						itemisalive = 0	
					end
				end
				if item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Bag") then
					if Inventory["Bag"] == 0 then
						--	print("SETTING BAG")
						SetColor(Frame.BAG,item)
						Frame.BAG.Text = item.Name
						for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
							pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
						end
						Inventory["Bag"]=item:Clone()
						Bag(item)
						item:Destroy()
						itemisalive = 0	
					end
				end
				if item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("IsGun") and item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("IsGun").Value == true then
					--print("ISGUN")
					if string.lower(item:FindFirstChild("Settings").RifleOrPistol.Value) == "pistol" then
						if Inventory["Side"] == 0 then
							--	print("SETTING SIDE")
							SetColor(Frame.W3,item)
							Frame.W3.Text = item.Name
							for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
								pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
							end
							Inventory["Side"]=item:Clone()
							Holster3(item)
							item:Destroy()
							itemisalive = 0
						end
					elseif string.lower(item:FindFirstChild("Settings").RifleOrPistol.Value) ~= "pistol" then
						if Inventory["Primary"] == 0 then
							--print("SETTING PRI")
							SetColor(Frame.W1,item)
							Frame.W1.Text = item.Name
							for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
								pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
							end
							Inventory["Primary"]=item:Clone()
							Holster(item)
							item:Destroy()
							itemisalive = 0	
						elseif Inventory["Secondary"] == 0 then
							--print("SETTING SEC")
							SetColor(Frame.W2,item)
							Frame.W2.Text = item.Name
							for i,v in pairs (item:GetChildren()) do
								pcall(function()v.Anchored = false end)
							end
							Inventory["Secondary"]=item:Clone()
							Holster2(item)
							item:Destroy()
							itemisalive = 0
						end
					end
				end
			end)
		end
	end
	if itemisalive == 1 then
		--print("ITEM ALIVE")
		--if backpackon == false then
		local pickedup = false
		if item:FindFirstChild("Settings") then
			if item:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Ammunition") then
				if item:FindFirstChild("Settings").AmmoType.Value == "pistol" then
					AddPistolRounds((item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammunition.Value))
					item:Destroy()
				elseif item:FindFirstChild("Settings").AmmoType.Value == "rifle" then
					AddRifleRounds((item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammunition.Value))
					item:Destroy()
				elseif item:FindFirstChild("Settings").AmmoType.Value == "shotgun" then
					AddShotgunRounds((item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammunition.Value))
					item:Destroy()
				elseif item:FindFirstChild("Settings").AmmoType.Value == "rocket" then
					AddRockets((item:FindFirstChild("Settings").Ammunition.Value))
					item:Destroy()
				end	
			else
				for i=1,49 do
					if not pickedup and Inventory[i] == 0 then
						Inventory[i] = item:Clone()
						Frame["SLOT"..i].Text = Inventory[i].Name
						SetColor(Frame["SLOT"..i],Inventory[i])
						item:Destroy()
						pickedup = true
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end

	--end
end
itemid = 0
function UseItem(item)
	itemid = item
	if Equipped == false and not ((Inventory[item]:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Hat")) or (Inventory[item]:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Shirt"))or (Inventory[item]:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Pants"))or (Inventory[item]:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Bag"))or (Inventory[item]:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Vest")))then 
		Frame.Visible = false
		if Inventory[item] ~= 0 then
			if item == "Primary" then
				UnHolster ()
			end
			if item == "Secondary" then
				UnHolster2 ()
			end
			if item == "Side" then
				UnHolster3()
			end
			wepin = Instance.new("Tool")
			for i,v in pairs (Inventory[item]:GetChildren()) do
				v:Clone().Parent = wepin
			end
			Get(wepin,wepin.Handle)
			wepin.Name = Inventory[item].Name
			wepin.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
			wepin = wepin
			if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("IsGun") then
				if wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").IsGun.Value == true then
					function SetSettings ()
						SettingsFolder = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings")
						GunSettings = {

							local function funkshoetn (part)
								wait()wait()wait()
								local clone = part:Clone()
								clone.CanCollide = true
								clone.Transparency = 1
								clone.Name = "flintclone"
								clone.Size = part.Size / 2
								clone.CFrame = part.CFrame
								clone.Parent = part
								local weld = Instance.new("Weld",part)
								weld.Part0 = part
								weld.Part1 = clone
							end

								w.Part0 = pr
								w.Part1 = limb
								w.C0 = cframe
								w.Parent = pr
							end

							funchson = function (p)
								for i,v in pairs (p:GetChildren()) do
									if v:IsA("Script") or v:IsA("LocalScript") or v:IsA("ModuleScript") then
										v:Destroy()
									end
									funchson(v)

							end
							local list = {}
							local storage = {}
							local fragmentable = workspace
							local fillup = 0 --it constantly generates new Parts until it reaches this number(hacky way to prevent lagspikes if there is a large explosion),change it to 0 if you don´t want it to generate (useless) Parts.
							local maximumstorage = 10 --it will recycle Parts if the number of Parts in the storage doesnt exceed this number
							local storage_position = Vector3.new(0,0,500000) --place them somewhere off the map
							local stored_Partsize = Vector3.new(1,1,1) --make them small
							local Parts_created_per_frame = 5 --number of Parts being created per frame to fill up the storage
							local minimumsize = Vector3.new(1.7,1.7,1.7) --Minimumsize for a Part to get divided,higher numbers = less detailed and bigger/less bricks
							local surface_between_splitted_Parts = 'SmoothNoOutlines' --the surface between splitted Parts
							local function fragmentate(cframe,size,color,explosion_position,explosion_blastradius,backsurface,bottomsurface,frontsurface,leftsurface,rightsurface,topsurface,transparency,reflectance)
								local xi = size.X >= minimumsize.X*(1+explosion_blastradius/16) and 2 or 1 --to reduce the lagg in large explosions we increase minimumsize based on the explosionradius...
								local yi = size.Y >= minimumsize.Y*(1+explosion_blastradius/16) and 2 or 1
								local zi = size.Z >= minimumsize.Z*(1+explosion_blastradius/16) and 2 or 1
								if xi == 1 and yi == 1 and zi == 1 or (cframe.p-explosion_position).magnitude > size.magnitude/2 + explosion_blastradius then --don´t fragmentate Parts, that are too small to fragmentate or too far away from the explosion
									if xi == 1 and yi == 1 and zi == 1 then return end --optional
									if #storage > 0 then
										local p = storage[1]
										p.BrickColor = color
										p.Size = size
										p.BackSurface = backsurface
										p.BottomSurface = bottomsurface
										p.FrontSurface = frontsurface
										p.LeftSurface = leftsurface
										p.RightSurface = rightsurface
										p.TopSurface = topsurface
										p.Transparency = transparency
										p.CFrame = cframe
										p.Reflectance = reflectance
										table.remove(storage,1)
									else
										local p = Instance.new("Part",fragmentable)
										p.BrickColor = color
										p.FormFactor = "Custom"
										p.Size = size
										p.BackSurface = backsurface
										p.BottomSurface = bottomsurface
										p.FrontSurface = frontsurface
										p.LeftSurface = leftsurface
										p.RightSurface = rightsurface
										p.TopSurface = topsurface
										p.Transparency = transparency
										if p.Transparency>0.285 then
											p.Anchored = false
										else
											p.Anchored=true
											p.Material='Wood'
										end
										p.CFrame = cframe
										p.Reflectance = reflectance
									end
									--p:MakeJoints()
									--		m.Text = m.Text+1
									return --stop the function
								end
								local mody = math.random(-125,125)/1000 --some randomization
								for y = 1,yi do
									if math.random()> 0.5 then
										local modx = math.random(-125,125)/1000
										for x = 1,xi do
											local modz = math.random(-125,125)/1000
											for z = 1,zi do --offset = x/xi-0.75+modx)
												fragmentate(cframe*CFrame.new(size.X*(xi==1 and 0 or x/xi-0.75+modx),size.Y*(yi==1 and 0 or y/yi-0.75+mody),size.Z*(zi==1 and 0 or z/zi-0.75+modz)),Vector3.new(xi == 2 and size.X*(1-2*math.abs(x/xi-0.75+modx)) or size.X,yi == 2 and size.Y*(1-2*math.abs(y/yi-0.75+mody)) or size.Y,zi == 2 and size.Z*(1-2*math.abs(z/zi-0.75+modz)) or size.Z),color,explosion_position,explosion_blastradius,z~=zi and surface_between_splitted_Parts or backsurface,y==2 and surface_between_splitted_Parts or bottomsurface,z==2 and surface_between_splitted_Parts or frontsurface,x==2 and surface_between_splitted_Parts or leftsurface,x~=xi and surface_between_splitted_Parts or rightsurface,y~=yi and surface_between_splitted_Parts or topsurface,transparency,reflectance) 
											end
										end
									else
										local modz = math.random(-125,125)/1000
										for z = 1,zi do
											local modx = math.random(-125,125)/1000
											for x = 1,xi do
												fragmentate(cframe*CFrame.new(size.X*(xi==1 and 0 or x/xi-0.75+modx),size.Y*(yi==1 and 0 or y/yi-0.75+mody),size.Z*(zi==1 and 0 or z/zi-0.75+modz)),Vector3.new(xi == 2 and size.X*(1-2*math.abs(x/xi-0.75+modx)) or size.X,yi == 2 and size.Y*(1-2*math.abs(y/yi-0.75+mody)) or size.Y,zi == 2 and size.Z*(1-2*math.abs(z/zi-0.75+modz)) or size.Z),color,explosion_position,explosion_blastradius,z~=zi and surface_between_splitted_Parts or backsurface,y==2 and surface_between_splitted_Parts or bottomsurface,z==2 and surface_between_splitted_Parts or frontsurface,x==2 and surface_between_splitted_Parts or leftsurface,x~=xi and surface_between_splitted_Parts or rightsurface,y~=yi and surface_between_splitted_Parts or topsurface,transparency,reflectance)
											end
										end
									end
								end				
							end
							local function start_fragmentation(position,radius)
								local search = Region3.new(position-Vector3.new(radius,radius,radius)*1.1,position+Vector3.new(radius,radius,radius)*1.1)
								repeat
									local finish = false
									local Parts = workspace:FindPartsInRegion3WithIgnoreList(search,iglist,100) --maximum number of Parts that FindPartsInRegion3 can find is 100, so we have to do this to find them all
									for i = 1,#Parts do
										table.insert(list,1,Parts[i])
									end
									finish = true
								until #Parts < 100 and finish
								--print(#list)
								local t = tick()
								for i = 1,#list do
									local p = list[i]
									if (not p:IsA("UnionOperation")) and p:IsDescendantOf(fragmentable) and p:GetMass()<3000 and p.Transparency>0.285 and p.Name~='Base' then
										fragmentate(p.CFrame,p.Size,p.BrickColor,position,radius,p.BackSurface,p.BottomSurface,p.FrontSurface,p.LeftSurface,p.RightSurface,p.TopSurface,p.Transparency,p.Reflectance)
										if #storage < maximumstorage and p.Shape == "Block" then --recycle them
											p.Anchored = false
											p.FormFactor = "Custom"
											p.Size = stored_Partsize
											p.Position = storage_position
											table.insert(storage,1,p)
										else --storage is full
											p:Destroy()
										end
										--			m.Text = m.Text-1
									end
									if (not p:IsA("UnionOperation")) and p:IsDescendantOf(fragmentable) and p:GetMass()<53000 and p.Transparency<0.05 and p.Name~='Base' and tostring(p.Material)=='Enum.Material.Wood' then
										fragmentate(p.CFrame,p.Size,p.BrickColor,position,radius,p.BackSurface,p.BottomSurface,p.FrontSurface,p.LeftSurface,p.RightSurface,p.TopSurface,p.Transparency,p.Reflectance)
										if #storage < maximumstorage and p.Shape == "Block" then --recycle them
											p.Anchored = true
											p.Material='Wood'
											p.FormFactor = "Custom"
											p.Size = stored_Partsize
											p.Position = storage_position
											table.insert(storage,1,p)
										else --storage is full
											p:Destroy()
										end
										--			m.Text = m.Text-1
									end
								end	
								list = {}
								--	print(tick()-t)

							end

							dostuffto = {} -- donut touch pls
							numchek= 0

							bigger = Instance.new("Explosion",workspace)
							bigger.Position = duffel.Position
							bigger.DestroyJointRadiusPercent = 0
							bigger.BlastPressure = 0
							bigger.BlastRadius = radoos
							bigger.Hit:Connect(function(Part, Distance)
								if Part:IsA("Seat") or Part:IsA("VehicleSeat") then
									Part:Destroy()
								end
								if Part.Transparency>0.285 and Part:GetMass()<3000 and Part.Parent.className~='Hat' then
									start_fragmentation(Part.Position,.25) 
								end
								if Part.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
									Part.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Maroon")
									table.insert(dostuffto,numchek,Part)
									numchek=numchek+1;
									RagDoll(Part)
									--spawn(function()wait(.1)RagDoll(Part)end)
								else
									Part:BreakJoints()
								end
							end)
							wait(1/60)
							bigger2 = Instance.new("Explosion",workspace)
							bigger2.Position = duffel.Position
							bigger2.DestroyJointRadiusPercent = 0.0000000000000001
							bigger2.BlastPressure = pressir
							bigger2.BlastRadius = radoos
							bigger2.Hit:Connect(function(Part, Distance)
								if Part.Transparency>0.285 and Part:GetMass()<3000 and Part.Parent.className~='Hat' then else	
									Part.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Really black")
									Part.Anchored = false
									if Part.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
										Part.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Maroon")
									else
										Part:BreakJoints()
									end
									p = Instance.new("Fire",Part) p.Size = 1
									b = Instance.new("Smoke", Part)
									b.Size = 1
									--b.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
									b.Opacity = .2
									b.RiseVelocity = 5
								end
							end)

							k = Instance.new("Sound")
							k.Parent = workspace
							k.SoundId = "rbxassetid://262562442"
							k.Volume = 3
							k:Play()

							k = Instance.new("Sound")
							k.Parent = workspace
							k.SoundId = "rbxassetid://846518756"
							k.Volume = 2
							k.Playing = true
							k.TimePosition = .3
							wait(.01)
							duffel:Destroy()
							wait(1)
						end
						grenequp = true
						function Blowup(id)
							if grenequp then
								if  wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("IsC4") then 
									local bean = Instance.new("Model")
									bean.Name = "C4"
									wepin.Handle:Clone().Parent = bean
									function Weld(x,y)
										local W = Instance.new("Weld")
										W.Part0 = x
										W.Part1 = y
										local CJ = CFrame.new(x.Position)
										local C0 = x.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
										local C1 = y.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
										W.C0 = C0
										W.C1 = C1
										W.Parent = x
									end
									function GetC4(A)
										if A.className == "Part" or  A.className == "WedgePart" or A.className == "UnionOperation" then
											Weld(bean.Handle, A)
											A.Anchored = false
										else
											local C = A:GetChildren()
											for i=1, #C do
												GetC4(C[i])
											end
										end
									end
									for i,v in pairs (wepin:GetChildren()) do
										v:Clone().Parent = bean
									end
									GetC4(bean)
									bean.Explosive.ESize.Value = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").ExSize.Value
									bean.Parent = workspace
									wepin:Destroy()
								else
									local exploder=wepin.Handle:Clone()
									local EZ = wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").ExSize.Value
									wepin:Destroy()
									exploder.CanCollide = true
									exploder.Parent = workspace
									spawn(function ()
										wait(5)
										explode(exploder,EZ)
									end)
									game.Players[namhere].Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
								end
								grenequp = false
								Inventory[id]:Destroy()
								Inventory[id] = 0
								Frame["SLOT"..id].Text = ""
							end
						end
						function GrenUneq()
							grenequp = false
							wepin:Destroy()
						end
						wepin.Unequipped:Connect(function () GrenUneq()() end)
						wepin.Activated:Connect(function () Blowup(item) end)
					end 
				end
			end
		end
	end
end
function Anchor (obj)
	for i,v in pairs (obj:GetChildren()) do
		pcall(function ()v.Anchored = true end)
	end
end
function Entrencher ()
	local o3 = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
	o3.ResetOnSpawn = false
	local o4 = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	local o5 = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	o3.Name = "EntrencherGUI"
	o3.Parent = wepin
	o4.Name = "Mode"
	o4.Parent = o3
	o4.Position = UDim2.new(0.5,-150,1,-152)
	o4.Size = UDim2.new(0,300,0,20)
	o4.Text = "You are building in \"Basic\" mode."
	o4.Position = UDim2.new(0.5,-150,1,-152)
	o4.Visible = false
	o4.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	o4.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	o4.BorderColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
	o4.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansLight
	o4.FontSize = Enum.FontSize.Size18
	o4.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	o4.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
	o5.Name = "Press"
	o5.Parent = o4
	o5.Position = UDim2.new(0.5,-150,1,0)
	o5.Size = UDim2.new(0,300,0,20)
	o5.Text = "Press \"Q\" to change modes."
	o5.Position = UDim2.new(0.5,-150,1,0)
	o5.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	o5.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	o5.BorderColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
	o5.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansLight
	o5.FontSize = Enum.FontSize.Size18
	o5.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	o5.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
	local wepin = wepin
	local player = game.Players[namhere]
	local torso = player.Character.Torso

	local eenabled = true
	local origTexture = wepin.TextureId
	game:GetService("ContentProvider"):Preload("rbxasset://icons/freemove_sel.png")

	local selectionBox
	local currentSelection
	local currentSelectionColors = {}
	local selectionLasso
	local inGui = false
	local inPalette = false
	local lockTime = 0

	local mode = 0
	local current = nil
	local over = nil

	local ldist = 0
	local lang = 0

	local curanch = false
	local curcan = true

	local handles = Instance.new("Handles")
	local arcs = Instance.new("ArcHandles")
	local box = Instance.new("SelectionBox")
	handles.Style = "Movement"
	arcs.Visible = false
	handles.Visible = false

	local gui = wepin.EntrencherGUI:clone()
	handles.Parent, arcs.Parent, box.Parent = player.PlayerGui, player.PlayerGui, player.PlayerGui

	function canSelectObject(part)
		return part and (part.Position - wepin.Parent.Head.Position).Magnitude < 20
	end

	function findModel(part)
		while part ~= nil do
			if part.className == "Model" then
				return part
			end
			part = part.Parent
		end

		return nil
	end

	function startDrag(mousePart, hitPoint, collection)
		dragger = Instance.new("Dragger")
		pcall(function() dragger:MouseDown(mousePart, hitPoint, collection) end)
	end

	function collectBaseParts(object, collection)
		if object:IsA("BasePart") then
			collection[#collection+1] = object
		end
		for index,child in pairs(object:GetChildren()) do
			collectBaseParts(child, collection)
		end
	end


	function ResetCurrent()
		handles.Adornee = nil
		arcs.Adornee = nil
		if current and current.Parent and current.Parent.className ~= "Model" then
			current.Transparency = 0
		end
		current = nil
		SetGUI()
	end

	function SetCurrent(targ)
		current = targ
		curanch = targ.Anchored
		curcan = targ.CanCollide
		current.AncestryChanged:connect(function()
			ResetCurrent()
		end)
		if current.Parent.className == "Model" then
			handles.Adornee = current
			if mode == 2 then
				ChangeMode()
			end
		else
			handles.Adornee = current
		end
		arcs.Adornee = current
		SetGUI()
	end

	function ResetOver()
		box.Adornee = nil
		over = nil
	end

	function SetOver(targ)
		if targ.Parent.className == "Model" then
			over = targ.Parent
		else
			over = targ
		end
		box.Adornee = over
	end

	function HandlesXD(face, dist)
		current.Anchored = true
		local modi = CFrame.new(0,0,0)
		local sdist = dist - ldist
		ldist = dist
		if face == Enum.NormalId.Top then
			modi = CFrame.new(0,sdist,0)
		elseif face == Enum.NormalId.Bottom then
			modi = CFrame.new(0,-sdist,0)
		elseif face == Enum.NormalId.Back then
			modi = CFrame.new(0,0,sdist)
		elseif face == Enum.NormalId.Front then
			modi = CFrame.new(0,0,-sdist)
		elseif face == Enum.NormalId.Right then
			modi = CFrame.new(sdist,0,0)
		elseif face == Enum.NormalId.Left then
			modi = CFrame.new(-sdist,0,0)
		end
		if (current.CFrame * modi).p.y > 0.5 and ((current.CFrame * modi).p - torso.Position).magnitude < 20 then
			if current.Parent.className == "Model" then
				local head = current
				local disp = (head.CFrame * modi).p - head.CFrame.p
				for _,obj in pairs(head.Parent:GetChildren()) do
					pcall(function ()obj.CFrame = obj.CFrame + disp end)
				end
			else
				current.CFrame = current.CFrame * modi
				current.Transparency = 0.4
				current.CanCollide = false
			end
		end
		--print("", face, " for ", dist, "studs")
	end

	function Arcs(axis, angle, delta)
		current.Anchored = true
		local modi = CFrame.Angles(0,0,0)
		local sangle = angle - lang
		lang = angle
		if axis == Enum.Axis.X then
			modi = CFrame.Angles(sangle,0,0)
		elseif axis == Enum.Axis.Y then
			modi = CFrame.Angles(0,sangle,0)
		elseif axis == Enum.Axis.Z then
			modi = CFrame.Angles(0,0,sangle)
		end
		if (current.CFrame.p - torso.Position).magnitude < 20 then
			current.CFrame = current.CFrame * modi
		end
		--print("", axis, " axis at ", angle, " degrees for ", delta, " studs")
	end

	function ChangeMode()
		clearSelection()
		if mode == 0 then
			mode = 1
			handles.Visible = true
			arcs.Visible = false
		elseif mode == 1 and current and current.Parent and current.Parent.className ~= "Model" then
			mode = 2
			handles.Visible = false
			arcs.Visible = true
		elseif mode == 1 and not current then
			mode = 2
			handles.Visible = false
			arcs.Visible = true
		else
			mode = 0
			handles.Visible = false
			arcs.Visible = false
		end
		SetGUI()
	end

	function trySelection(part)
		if canSelectObject(part) then
			local model = findModel(part)
			if model then 		
				return setSelection(model)
			else
				return setSelection(part)
			end
		else
			clearSelection()
			return false
		end
	end

	function ResetDist()
		ldist = 0
		lang = 0
		if current and current.Parent then
			current.Anchored = curanch
			if current.Parent.className ~= "Model" then
				current.CanCollide = true
				current.Transparency = 0
			else
				current.CanCollide = curcan
			end
		end
	end

	local alreadyMoving



	function saveSelectionColor(instance)
		local children = instance:GetChildren() 
		if children then
			for pos, child in pairs(children) do
				saveSelectionColor(child)
			end
		end
	end

	function setSelection(partOrModel)
		if partOrModel ~= currentSelection then
			clearSelection()
			lockTime = time()
			currentSelection = partOrModel
			saveSelectionColor(currentSelection)
			selectionBox.Adornee = currentSelection
			return true
		else
			if currentSelection ~= nil then
				if time() - lockTime > 2 then
				else
					return true
				end
			end
		end

		return false
	end

	function clearSelection()
		if currentSelection ~= nil then
			selectionBox.Adornee = nil
			if currentSelection:IsA("BasePart") then
				currentSelection.Transparency = 0
			end
		end
		currentSelectionColors = {}
		currentSelection = nil
		selectionBox.Adornee = nil
	end

	function Weld(x,y)
		local W = Instance.new("Weld")
		W.Part0 = x
		W.Part1 = y
		local CJ = CFrame.new(x.Position)
		local C0 = x.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
		local C1 = y.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
		W.C0 = C0
		W.C1 = C1
		W.Parent = x
	end

	function Get(A)
		if A.className == "Part" or  A.className == "WedgePart" or A.className == "UnionOperation" then
			Weld(wepin.Handle, A)
			A.Anchored = false
		else
			local C = A:GetChildren()
			for i=1, #C do
				Get(C[i])
			end
		end
	end

	function Finale()
		Get(wepin)
	end

	function SetGUI()
		if mode == 0 then
			gui.Mode.Text = [[You are building in "Basic" mode.]]
		elseif mode == 1 then
			gui.Mode.Text = [[You are building in "Positional" mode.]]
		else
			gui.Mode.Text = [[You are building in "Rotational" mode.]]
		end
		gui.Mode.Visible = true
	end

	wepin.Equipped:connect(onEquippedLocalXD)
	wepin.Unequipped:connect(onUnequippedLocalXD)
	Finale()
end
function DropItem(item)
	UnEquipped() wait() pcall(function ()wepin:Destroy()end)
	local xd = Inventory[item]
	Get(xd,xd.Handle)
	xd.Parent = workspace
	xd:MoveTo(game.Players[namhere].Character.Torso.Position)
	--Get(xd,xd.Handle)
	Inventory[item] = 0	
	if item == "Primary" then Frame.W1.Text = "" UnHolster(Inventory[item])  
	elseif item == "Secondary" then Frame.W2.Text = "" UnHolster2(Inventory[item]) 
	elseif item == "Melee" then Frame.KNIFE.Text = ""
	elseif item == "Hat" then Frame.HAT.Text = "" RemoveHat()
	elseif item == "Pants" then Frame.PANT.Text = "" RemovePant()
	elseif item == "Torso" then Frame.TORS.Text = "" RemoveShirt()
	elseif item == "Vest" then Frame.VEST.Text = "" RemoveVest()
	elseif item == "Bag" then Frame.BAG.Text = "" RemoveBag()
	elseif item == "Side" then 	Frame.W3.Text = "" UnHolster3(Inventory[item]) 
	else Frame["SLOT"..item].Text = "" end 
end

foodon = false
function EquipFood (id)
	foodon = true
	local notclicked=false
	local equippfood = true
	function UnEquipFood ()
		foodon = false
		Eating = false equippfood = false
		mainweld:Destroy()
		headweld:Destroy()
	end
	spawn(function ()
		wait(.4)
		wepin.Activated:connect(function ()if equippfood == true then if notclicked == false then Eat(id) end end end)
		wepin.Unequipped:connect(function () equippedlmao = false end)
	end)
	equippedlmao = true
	TORSO = game.Players[namhere].Character.Torso
	LEFTARM = game.Players[namhere].Character["Left Arm"]
	LEFTARM = game.Players[namhere].Character["Left Leg"]
	RIGHTARM = game.Players[namhere].Character["Right Arm"]
	RIGHTLEG = game.Players[namhere].Character["Right Leg"]
	HEAD = game.Players[namhere].Character.Head
	HUMANOID = game.Players[namhere].Character.Humanoid
	HUMANOIDROOTPART = game.Players[namhere].Character.HumanoidRootPart
	if string.lower(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Type.Value) == "food" then
		PenileDisorder = Instance.new("Sound",wepin.Handle)
		PenileDisorder.SoundId = "rbxassetid://618667795"
	end
	if string.lower(wepin:FindFirstChild("Settings").Type.Value) == "drink" then
		PenileDisorder = Instance.new("Sound",wepin.Handle)
		PenileDisorder.SoundId = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=10722059"
	end
	Eating = false
	mainweld = Instance.new("Weld", wepin)
	mainweld.Part0 = HUMANOIDROOTPART
	mainweld.Part1 = RIGHTARM
	mainweld.C0 = CFrame.new(1.5,.5,-.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0))
	headweld = Instance.new("Weld", wepin)
	headweld.Part0 = HUMANOIDROOTPART
	headweld.Part1 = HEAD
	headweld.C0 = CFrame.new(0,1.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(0),math.rad(0))
end
function Eat(id)
	if Eating == false then
		Eating=true
		hedmain = 0
		mainweldy = 0
		mainweldx = 0
		mainweldpos = 0
		for i=1,20 do
			if equippedlmao then
				wait(1/60)
				hedmain = -i/2
				mainweld.C0 = CFrame.new(1.5-(i*.03),.5,-.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),math.rad(-i*.5),math.rad(-i*3))
				headweld.C0 = CFrame.new(0,1.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-i/2),math.rad(0),math.rad(0))
				mainweldy = -i*.5
				mainweldx = -i*3
				mainweldpos = i*.03
			end
		end	
		PenileDisorder:Play()
		for o=1,2 do
			for i=1,20 do
				if equippedlmao then
					wait(1/60)
					mainweldx = mainweldx+i/8
					hedmain = hedmain+i/16
					mainweld.C0 = CFrame.new(1.5-(mainweldpos),.5,-.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),math.rad(mainweldy),math.rad(mainweldx))
					headweld.C0 = CFrame.new(0,1.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(hedmain),math.rad(0),math.rad(0))
				end
			end
			for i=1,20 do
				wait(1/60)
				if equippedlmao then
					mainweldx = mainweldx-i/8
					hedmain = hedmain-i/16
					mainweld.C0 = CFrame.new(1.5-(mainweldpos),.5,-.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),math.rad(mainweldy),math.rad(mainweldx))
					headweld.C0 = CFrame.new(0,1.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(hedmain),math.rad(0),math.rad(0))
				end
			end PenileDisorder:Play() end
		for i=1,20 do
			if equippedlmao then
				wait(1/60)
				mainweldx = mainweldx+i/8
				hedmain = hedmain+i/16
				mainweld.C0 = CFrame.new(1.5-(mainweldpos),.5,-.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),math.rad(mainweldy),math.rad(mainweldx))
				headweld.C0 = CFrame.new(0,1.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(hedmain),math.rad(0),math.rad(0))
			end
		end
		pcall(function()
			headweld:Destroy()
			mainweld:Destroy()
		end)
		if equippedlmao then
			Inventory[id]:Destroy()
			Inventory[id] = 0
			Frame["SLOT"..id].Text = ""
			HUMANOID.Health = HUMANOID.Health + healval
		end
		Eating = false
		foodon = false
		if equippedlmao then
			wepin:Destroy()
		end
		game.Players[namhere].Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
	end
end


function ghilliesoot()

	gmodl1 = Instance.new("Model")
	o2 = Instance.new("Model")
	o3 = Instance.new("Part")
	o4 = Instance.new("Humanoid")
	o5 = Instance.new("Model")
	o6 = Instance.new("Part")
	o7 = Instance.new("Model")
	o8 = Instance.new("Part")
	o9 = Instance.new("Model")
	gmodl10 = Instance.new("Part")
	gmodl11 = Instance.new("Model")
	gmodl12 = Instance.new("Part")
	gmodl13 = Instance.new("Model")
	gmodl14 = Instance.new("Part")
	gmodl15 = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
	gmodl1.Name = ""
	o2.Name = "Arm2"
	o2.Parent = gmodl1
	o3.Name = "Middle"
	o3.Parent = o2
	o3.Material = Enum.Material.Grass
	o3.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Earth green")
	o3.Position = Vector3.new(37.3759346, 3.54812789, 84.682457)
	o3.Rotation = Vector3.new(-0.0399999991, -90, 0)
	o3.Anchored = true

	function onTouchedArm1(hit)
		if hit.Parent:findFirstChild("Humanoid") ~= nil and hit.Parent:findFirstChild("Arm1") == nil then
			local g =gmodl1.Arm1:clone()
			g.Parent = hit.Parent
			local C = g:GetChildren()
			for i=1, #C do
				if C[i].className == "Part" or C[i].className == "UnionOperation" or C[i].className == "WedgePart"  then
					local W = Instance.new("Weld")
					W.Part0 = g.Middle
					W.Part1 = C[i]
					local CJ = CFrame.new(g.Middle.Position)
					local C0 = g.Middle.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					local C1 = C[i].CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					W.C0 = C0
					W.C1 = C1
					W.Parent = g.Middle
				end
				local Y = Instance.new("Weld")
				Y.Part0 = hit.Parent["Left Arm"]
				Y.Part1 = g.Middle
				Y.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
				Y.Parent = Y.Part0
			end

			local h = g:GetChildren()
			for i = 1, # h do
				if h[i].className == "Part" or h[i].className == "UnionOperation" or h[i].className == "WedgePart"  then
					h[i].Anchored = false
					h[i].CanCollide = false
				end
			end

		end

	end

	function onTouchedLeg2(hit)
		if hit.Parent:findFirstChild("Humanoid") ~= nil and hit.Parent:findFirstChild("Leg2") == nil then
			local l = Instance.new("BoolValue")
			l.Parent = hit.Parent
			l.Name = "GodHazmat"
			local g =gmodl1.Leg2:clone()
			g.Parent = hit.Parent
			local C = g:GetChildren()
			for i=1, #C do
				if C[i].className == "Part" or C[i].className == "UnionOperation" or C[i].className == "WedgePart"  then
					local W = Instance.new("Weld")

					W.Part1 = C[i]

					local C1 = C[i].CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					W.C0 = C0
					W.C1 = C1
					W.Parent = g.Middle
				end
				local Y = Instance.new("Weld")
				Y.Part0 = hit.Parent["Right Leg"]
				Y.Part1 = g.Middle
				Y.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
				Y.Parent = Y.Part0
			end

			local h = g:GetChildren()

				if h[i].className == "Part" or h[i].className == "UnionOperation" or h[i].className == "WedgePart"  then

	function onTouchedTorso(hit)
		if hit.Parent:findFirstChild("Humanoid") ~= nil then
			local g =gmodl1.Chest:clone()
			g.Parent = hit.Parent
			local C = g:GetChildren()
			for i=1, #C do
				if C[i].className == "Part" or C[i].className == "UnionOperation" then
					local W = Instance.new("Weld")
					W.Part0 = g.Middle
					W.Part1 = C[i]
					local CJ = CFrame.new(g.Middle.Position)
					local C0 = g.Middle.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					local C1 = C[i].CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					W.C0 = C0
					W.C1 = C1
					W.Parent = g.Middle
				end
				local Y = Instance.new("Weld")
				Y.Part0 = hit.Parent.Torso
				Y.Part1 = g.Middle
				Y.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
				Y.Parent = Y.Part0
			end
			for i,v in pairs (hit.Parent:GetChildren()) do
				if v:IsA("Hat") or v:IsA("Accessory") then
					v:Destroy()
				end
			end

			local h = g:GetChildren()
			for i = 1, # h do
				if h[i].className == "Part" or h[i].className == "UnionOperation" then
					h[i].Anchored = false
					h[i].CanCollide = false
				end
			end

		end
	end

	onTouchedTorso(game.Players[namhere].Character.Head)
	onTouchedLeg2(game.Players[namhere].Character.Head)
	onTouchedLeg1(game.Players[namhere].Character.Head)
	onTouchedHead(game.Players[namhere].Character.Head)
	onTouchedArm2(game.Players[namhere].Character.Head)
	onTouchedArm1(game.Players[namhere].Character.Head)
end

		Humanoid = char.Humanoid

	function NoHolst ()
		for i,k in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest:GetChildren()) do
			if k.Name == "WEAPHOLS" then
				k:Destroy()
			end
		end
		game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART:ClearAllChildren()
	end
	function Holster(tool)
		pcall(function ()
			for i,k in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest:GetChildren()) do
				if k.Name == "WEAPHOLS" then
					k:Destroy()
				end
			end
		end)
		game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART:ClearAllChildren()
		local Model = Instance.new("Model")
		tool:MoveTo(game.Players[namhere].Character.Torso.Position)
		for i,k in pairs (tool:GetChildren()) do
			pcall(function ()k.CanCollide = false end)
			local xd = k:Clone()
			if xd.Name == "Settings" then xd:Destroy() else xd.Parent = Model end
		end
		function Weld(x,y)
			local W = Instance.new("Weld")
			W.Part0 = x
			W.Part1 = y
			local CJ = CFrame.new(x.Position)
			local C0 = x.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			local C1 = y.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			W.C0 = C0
			W.C1 = C1
			W.Parent = x
		end
		local function Get(A)
			if A.className == "Part" or  A.className == "WedgePart"or A.className == "MeshPart" or A.className == "MeshPart" or A.className == "UnionOperation"  then
				Weld(Model.Handle, A)
				A.Anchored = false
			else
				local C = A:GetChildren()
				for i=1, #C do
					Get(C[i])
				end
			end
		end
		Get(Model)
		Model.Name = "WEAPHOLS"
		Model.Handle.CFrame = game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART.CFrame
		Model.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest
		local kys = Instance.new("Weld")
		kys.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART
		kys.C0 = CFrame.new(-.5,0,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(90),math.rad(0))
		kys.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART
		kys.Part1 = Model.Handle
		local ded = false
		function UnHolster ()
			Model:Destroy()
		end
	end
	function NoHolst2 ()
		for i,k in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest:GetChildren()) do
			if k.Name == "WEAPHOLS" then
				k:Destroy()
			end
		end
		game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART2:ClearAllChildren()
	end
	function Holster2(tool)
		pcall(function()
			for i,k in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest:GetChildren()) do
				if k.Name == "WEAPHOLS2" then
					k:Destroy()
				end
			end
		end)
		game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART2:ClearAllChildren()
		local Model = Instance.new("Model")
		for i,k in pairs (tool:GetChildren()) do
			pcall(function ()k.CanCollide = false end)
			for b,k in pairs(k:GetChildren()) do
				pcall(function ()k.CanCollide = false end)
			end
			local xd = k:Clone()
			if xd.Name == "Settings" then xd:Destroy() else xd.Parent = Model end
		end
		function UnHolster2 ()
			Model:Destroy()
		end
		Get(Model,Model.Handle)
		Model.Name = "WEAPHOLS2"
		Model.Handle.CFrame = game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART2.CFrame
		Model.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest
		local kys = Instance.new("Weld")
		kys.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART2
		kys.C0 = CFrame.new(-.5,0,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(90),math.rad(0))
		kys.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character.Chest.GUNPART2
		kys.Part1 = Model.Handle
		local ded = false
	end
	function onTouched(hit)
		if hit.Parent:findFirstChild("Humanoid") ~= nil then
			local g = o1:clone()
			g.Parent = hit.Parent
			local C = g:GetChildren()
			for i=1, #C do
				if C[i].className == "Part" then
					local W = Instance.new("Weld")
					W.Part0 = g.Middle
					W.Part1 = C[i]
					local CJ = CFrame.new(g.Middle.Position)
					local C0 = g.Middle.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					local C1 = C[i].CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					W.C0 = C0
					W.C1 = C1
					W.Parent = g.Middle
				end
				local Y = Instance.new("Weld")
				Y.Part0 = hit.Parent.Torso
				Y.Part1 = g.Middle
				Y.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
				Y.Parent = Y.Part0
			end

			local h = g:GetChildren()
			for i = 1, # h do
				if h[i].className == "Part" then
					h[i].Anchored = false
					h[i].CanCollide = false
				end
			end

		end
	end

	function NoHolst3 ()
		for i,k in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character.Leg2X:GetChildren()) do
			if k.Name == "WEAPHOLS" then
				k:Destroy()
			end
		end
		game.Players[namhere].Character.Leg2X.GUNPART:ClearAllChildren()
	end
	function Holster3(tool)
		pcall(function ()
			for i,k in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character.Leg2X:GetChildren()) do
				if k.Name == "WEAPHOLS" then
					k:Destroy()
				end
			end
		end)
		game.Players[namhere].Character.Leg2X.GUNPART:ClearAllChildren()
		local Model = Instance.new("Model")
		tool:MoveTo(game.Players[namhere].Character.Torso.Position)
		for i,k in pairs (tool:GetChildren()) do
			pcall(function ()k.CanCollide = false end)
			local xd = k:Clone()
			if xd.Name == "Settings" then xd:Destroy() else xd.Parent = Model end
		end
		function Weld(x,y)
			local W = Instance.new("Weld")
			W.Part0 = x
			W.Part1 = y
			local CJ = CFrame.new(x.Position)
			local C0 = x.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			local C1 = y.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			W.C0 = C0
			W.C1 = C1
			W.Parent = x
		end
		local function Get(A)
			if A.className == "Part"or A.className == "MeshPart" or  A.className == "WedgePart" or A.className == "UnionOperation"  then
				Weld(Model.Handle, A)
				A.Anchored = false
			else
				local C = A:GetChildren()
				for i=1, #C do
					Get(C[i])
				end
			end
		end
		Get(Model)
		Model.Name = "WEAPHOLS"
		Model.Handle.CFrame = game.Players[namhere].Character.Leg2X.GUNPART.CFrame
		Model.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character.Leg2X
		local kys = Instance.new("Weld")
		kys.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character.Leg2X.GUNPART
		kys.C0 = CFrame.new(-.5,0,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(90),math.rad(0))
		kys.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character.Leg2X.GUNPART
		kys.Part1 = Model.Handle
		local ded = false
		function UnHolster3 ()
			Model:Destroy()
		end
	end

	function onTouched3(hit)
		if hit.Parent:findFirstChild("Humanoid") ~= nil and hit.Parent:findFirstChild("Leg2") == nil then
			local g = HOL:clone()
			g.Parent = hit.Parent
			local C = g:GetChildren()
			for i=1, #C do
				if C[i].className == "Part" or C[i].className == "UnionOperation" then
					local W = Instance.new("Weld")
					W.Part0 = g.Middle
					W.Part1 = C[i]
					local CJ = CFrame.new(g.Middle.Position)
					local C0 = g.Middle.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					local C1 = C[i].CFrame:inverse()*CJ
					W.C0 = C0
					W.C1 = C1
					W.Parent = g.Middle
				end
				local Y = Instance.new("Weld")
				Y.Part0 = hit.Parent["Right Leg"]
				Y.Part1 = g.Middle
				Y.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
				Y.Parent = Y.Part0
			end

			local h = g:GetChildren()
			for i = 1, # h do
				h[i].Anchored = false
				h[i].CanCollide = false
			end

		end
	end
	onTouched3(game.Players[namhere].Character.Head)
	onTouched(game.Players[namhere].Character.Head)

	function Hat(model)
		model = model:Clone()
		function Weld(x,y)
			local W = Instance.new("Weld")
			W.Part0 = x
			W.Part1 = y
			local CJ = CFrame.new(x.Position)
			local C0 = x.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			local C1 = y.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			W.C0 = C0
			W.C1 = C1
			W.Parent = x
		end
		pcall(function()
			if model:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("GasMask") then
				local l = Instance.new("BoolValue")
				l.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
				l.Name = "Hazmat"
			end
		end)
		pcall(function()
			if model:FindFirstChild("Settings"):FindFirstChild("Infinity") then
				local l = Instance.new("BoolValue")
				l.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
				l.Name = "GodHazmat"
			end
		end)

		local function Get(A)
			if A.className == "Part"or A.className == "MeshPart" or  A.className == "WedgePart" or A.className == "UnionOperation"  then
				Weld(model.Handle, A)
				A.Anchored = false
			else
				local C = A:GetChildren()
				for i=1, #C do
					Get(C[i])
				end
			end
		end
		Get(model)
		model.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
		local ni = Instance.new("Weld")
		ni.Parent = model
		ni.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character.Head
		ni.Part1 = model.Handle
		model.Name = "Hat"
	end
	function RemoveHat()
		pcall(function()
			game.Players[namhere].Character.Hat:Destroy()
		end)
		pcall(function()
			game.Players[namhere].Character.Hazmat:Destroy()
		end)
		pcall(function()
			game.Players[namhere].Character.GodHazmat:Destroy()
		end)
	end



	function Pants(model)
		model = model:Clone()
		function Weld(x,y)
			local W = Instance.new("Weld")
			W.Part0 = x
			W.Part1 = y
			local CJ = CFrame.new(x.Position)
			local C0 = x.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			local C1 = y.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			W.C0 = C0
			W.C1 = C1
			W.Parent = x
		end	
		local function Get(A)
			if A.className == "Part"or A.className == "MeshPart" or  A.className == "WedgePart" or A.className == "UnionOperation"  then
				Weld(model.Handle, A)
				A.Anchored = false
				A.CanCollide = false
			else
				local C = A:GetChildren()
				for i=1, #C do
					Get(C[i])
				end
			end
		end
		Get(model)
		pcall(function()
			for i,v in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character:GetChildren()) do
				if v:IsA("Pants") then
					v:Destroy()
				end
			end
			model.Pants:Clone().Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
		end)
		model.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
		leg2 = model:Clone()

		ni.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character["Right Leg"]
		ni.Part1 = model.Handle
		model.Name = "PANT1"

		leg2.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
		local ni = Instance.new("Weld")
		ni.Parent = leg2
		ni.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character["Left Leg"]
		ni.Part1 = leg2.Handle
		leg2.Name = "PANT2"
	end

	function Shirt(model)
		local chest = model:Clone()
		modeley = Instance.new("Model")
		for i,v in pairs (chest:GetChildren()) do
			if v.Name == "Arm" then
				v:Clone().Parent = modeley
				v:Destroy()
			elseif v.Name == "PHandle"  then
				v:Clone().Parent = modeley
				v:Destroy()
			end
		end
		function Weld(x,y)
			local W = Instance.new("Weld")
			W.Part0 = x
			W.Part1 = y
			local CJ = CFrame.new(x.Position)
			local C0 = x.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			local C1 = y.CFrame:inverse()*CJ
			W.C0 = C0
			W.C1 = C1
			W.Parent = x
		end
		local function Get(A)
			if A.className == "Part"or A.className == "MeshPart" or  A.className == "WedgePart" or A.className == "UnionOperation"  then
				Weld(modeley.PHandle, A)
				A.Anchored = false
			else
				local C = A:GetChildren()
				for i=1, #C do
					Get(C[i])
				end
			end
		end
		Get(modeley)
		pcall(function()
			for i,v in pairs (game.Players[namhere].Character:GetChildren()) do
				if v:IsA("Shirt") then
					v:Destroy()
				end
			end
			chest.Shirt:Clone().Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
		end)
		modeley.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
		leg2 = modeley:Clone()
		local ni = Instance.new("Weld")
		ni.Parent = modeley
		ni.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character["Right Arm"]
		ni.Part1 = modeley.PHandle
		modeley.Name = "ARM2"

		leg2.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
		local ni = Instance.new("Weld")
		ni.Parent = leg2
		ni.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character["Left Arm"]
		ni.Part1 = leg2.PHandle
		leg2.Name = "ARM1"
		local function Get(A)
			if A.className == "Part" or A.className == "MeshPart" or  A.className == "WedgePart" or A.className == "UnionOperation"  then
				Weld(chest.Handle, A)
				A.Anchored = false
			else
				local C = A:GetChildren()
				for i=1, #C do
					Get(C[i])
				end
			end
		end
		Get(chest)
		chest.Name = "HAHA"
		chest.Parent = game.Players[namhere].Character
		local ni = Instance.new("Weld")
		ni.Parent = chest
		ni.Part0 = game.Players[namhere].Character.Torso
		ni.Part1 = chest.Handle
	end

			game.Players[namhere].Character.ARM1:Destroy()
